This time I finally had the opportunity to experience it (I am used to staying at Marriott, InterContinental, Hilton, and Sheraton). I stayed for 2 nights and liked the overall environment, which was very retro and court-style, but the overall service did not meet my expectations. Maybe it was my first time staying there, and I was a Ctrip customer. I did not enjoy much attention from the service, especially when solving problems, I was more hasty, perfunctory, and rushed. (For example, the extension of stay was changed to refund + new stay; the deposit was refunded only after I called to inform that it had not been refunded 2 days after leaving the hotel). But there are also good things: for example, masks are provided (Wangfujing Hilton and Novotel Peace do not provide them). In fact, the services of many high-end chain hotels in China have surpassed those of international brands, such as Atour and Jianguo. I will stay at the Ritz again if I have the chance, because I like the JING tea I drink at breakfast.
